So, why messaging matters in 2025 in

from an alum,

from a pile of 500

A referral can move your application
from a pile of 500 to the top 10

often skim LinkedIn on their phone
between meetings.

individuals. And then, of course, taking
the technical uh interview.
The soft skills help you pass the
interview loop and keep the job once you
land it.
So, both are essential. Tech is a team
sport. So what's the difference? What is
hard skills versus soft skills? Well,
the hard skills, they are what you can
do,
right? So these are technical teachable
abilities usually learned through
training courses or hands-on experience.
They're easy to measure and often show
up in job description and LinkedIn uh
skills lists, which is why it's
important that these skills are matching
up with the job descriptions of
positions that you're applying to. So
for example for developers you've got
JavaScript react NodeJS git GitHub REST

things those everything I've listed,

skills, the the tools that you use every
single day, and they're the tools in
your toolbox. They show what you can
build.
Now, conversely, you've got the soft
